<Author>justfrank
<Content>Excellent small hotel My wife and i recently spent 9 nights at Banks Mansion. It was a great choice for a long stay, because everyone at the hotel goes out of their way to make you feel like you're in a home away from home.Upon our early morning arrival, the room we'd reserved was still occupied. The desk clerk asked if we'd like to try a different room. We agreed, but soon after that decided we'd like something else (all of the rooms are different). Even so, they let us sleep in the room we weren't keeping for 3 hours before moving us to our actual room. I've never encountered hospitality like that.Our room (210) was spacious, quiet and pleasant, if a bit dark. The bed was comfortable and the A/C kept the desired temperature. The bathroom was lovely. There is a complimentary minibar that they will stock with almost anything you ask for, and in the lobby there's complimentary beverages and snacks 24 hours a day. The breakfast room was very hot, but the food was good. The location is on a canal near Rembrandtplein, and it was no more than a 10 minute walk to all of the major tourist sites, and the tram runs right by the hotel.Everything about our stay was excellent, but what made it special was the caring, attentive staff that bent over backwards to help us at every turn.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Seams were showing a tad... My husband and I stayed here July 5 - July 12. It's a nice property to be sure and well located. And the concept of the upscale freebies in the lobby and in-room mini bar are great in theory. These services appeared however to break down over the weekend and things were not all replaced in the room or lobby bar. Items were left unrefilled for extended periods of time. The decanters of vodka, whiskey, gin etc for instance were left emptyfor a full day. The Bar aspect of this area is really pretty marginal. The lobby area was also littered with bottles, cups, wrappers for extended periods. Staff is pleasant, very young and perhaps a little lacking in supervision. Room nice but tiny. Dusting is not a priority with the maids nor is cleaning mirrors. There also was a mysterious loud booming noise (doors slamming?) we had to hear through the day and night. Not enough to keep you awake but there.The AC was an absolute must during this period -- and the room was nice and chilled. The common areas on the other hand were very very warm at all times.I think we would try another hotel if we go back. Those complimentary items and great but only if they are really delivered on; otherwise, just stay elsewhere and pay for them.

<Author>Quatchman
<Content>Fantastic ! Stayed here with my wife for 3 nights at the beginning of July. The hotel is ideally situated and in walking distance to all the main areas. The reviews that I read before we travelled are spot on; this is a great hotel and I would highly recommend it.We used the Connexions shuttle service located at A7 at the airport. Took around 20mins to get to the hotel at a cost of 12 euros each which I didn't think was bad when you consider it drops you right outside the hotel. Will use the tram and train to return just for a different experience. Apparantly the train to the airport runs every 15 minutes and the tram can be picked up about 50m from the hotel.The staff are extremely helpful with plenty of knowledge about the area and things to do and see. The room which features the complimantary minibar was great, a good size and extremely clean and well presented. It was very hot when we stayed and the air-con was a welcome relief from the heat of the streets.The addition of the complimantry bar in the lounge together with snacks and sweets was also a real plus together with the free internet access on which i'm writing the review right now!We were recommended the Dynasty chinese restaurant by the staff who based their advice not only on having visited their themselves but also with the aid of the trusty restaurant guide book they have behind the counter with ratings based on customer experiences. We paid 90 euros for the 2 of us; not cheap but the food and service was exceptional. If the weather is good ask for a table in the rear courtyard garden which is very pretty and away from the hustle and bustle with a great atmosphere.We did what I imagine are the usual museum visits including the Anne Frank house which is about a 25min walk from the hotel. Don't be fooled by what appears to be a queue that stretches round the corner. It moves pretty quick and once inside there is plenty of space to walk around freely. Pretty poignant stuff. Keep your wits about you in the Red Light District and ignore the the drug dealers and you'll be fine.Overall, we had a great time and would highly recommended the Banks Mansion !

<Author>MarkkuOulu
<Content>Wonderful Stayed there 3 nights with my wife.Great location between the busy city and more relaxed quarters with antique shops, galleries and good restaurants. We didn't need any transportation during our stay due to the location (visited e.g. Rijksmuseum, Anne Frank Huis and Oude Kerk).Very friendly staff.The room was small on US standards, but big enough for a few nights stay.For dinner experience visit Pasta e Basta with singing waiters / waitresses. If you fancy large 5 star hotels, this is not your place. If you would like to stay in a smaller place with cozy home feeling, this definitely is your place.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>What a gem! Have just returned from a 2 night stay which was a birthday treat for my mum. And we had a fantastic time. We go away every year together for a short break and the Banks Mansion is definitely the best hotel we have stayed at! It wasn't cheap, however it was well worth the money for all the 'extras'. Free drinks both in room and 'living' area, free internet, great breakfast, dvds etc.. I have just read the review of the american couple who complained and said it was the worse service they've ever experienced. Well, I find this seriously hard to believe. Were they really staying in the same hotel???? We found the staff extremely attentive and helpful and obliging to every request. And everything with a smile! And everything really has been well thought out in the rooms... right down to the 'pillow menu' to ensure that you get a good nights sleep! The location is also great and having now stayed at the Banks Mansion I can't imagine wanting to stay at another hotel in Amsterdam when I go back next! Incidentally, we also went to a lovely restaurant called Zuid Zeeland - just about 100m along the herengacht canal. It wasn't cheap, but service and food were both excellent. We also tried Gaucho on Dam Trak and although neither of us are big meat eaters and were initially a bit put off about eating in an Argentinian restaurant, they don't just serve steak! And the food was very good and reasonable value, especially considering the location.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>The Worst Service in the Hotel Industry My husband and I had booked a room for four nights on our first trip to Amsterdam. We booked a room months in advance at the rate of 235 Euros per night. Upon arrival, there is no one to assist with your bags (with multiple employees at the front desk watching us struggle with our luggage) and only stairs to gain access to the lobby. Upon check-in we were assigned a room one level about the street facing the street. We asked if there was a room on a higher floor, we were given the option of a smoking room in the back of the hotel. We chose the non-smoking room. Needless to say, the street facing room was extremely noisy and I did not sleep the entire first night . You feel as if you are sleeping on the sidewalk. When I politely asked to switch rooms the following morning while offering to pay for an upgrade to a canal facing room towards the back of the hotel, I was offered a room on the corner of the street and canal one floor higher, that was a smoking room. The front desk employees were rude and appeared bothered by my request and explained that had very few rooms to offer. However, during this short period of time, several couples walked into the hotel and inquired about rooms and were told they had several rooms available. I happily moved my items to a smoking room with non-functioning air conditioning. I once again contacted the front desk and they assured me it could be fixed. After calling twice, an employee came to fix the air conditioning and to our dismay, five hours later still had no air conditioning. The rude and incompetent woman at the front desk assured me there was nothing they could do and it would be cooler in Amsterdam in two more days. They had no other rooms for us and what was the big deal. At this point, we packed our bags and moved hotels. When our friends arrived a half hour later, they were offered the suite during their stay but had booked a room at the same rate we had paid the night before.The staff is rude, inexperienced and on several occasions, I witnessed them barking at other hotel guests. They have no interest in answering questions, assisting with sightseeing inquiries and do not help with luggage or obtaining taxis. Overall, this was the worst service I have ever experienced. I would highly recommend the Hotel Pulitzer.

<Author>gilliani
<Content>gorgeous hotel.....so cosy! My boyfriend and I stayed here in December last year as a last minute break. We booked directly through the hotels website as this was the best price....contrary to what we had read on various travel company sites! We arrived at the hotel at around 10.30pm but had let the hotel know that our flight didn't arrive till late...they were very friendly and helpful and didn't seem hassled by our late arrival. We ended up getting the train to the centre of amsterdam as the shuttle bus was very expensive and told us it did not pass our hotel....even though the sign said it did! The hotel room was really clean and well decorated though was not the hugest room it was fine for the two of us. The beds are comfortable and you have a choice of pillows. The tv is plasma screen- wall mounted and the movies/ all channels are free.  The mini bar in the room is well stocked with lager,coke,diet coke,fruit juices,water and you have large decanters of brandy,whisky and gin too. We drank much of this on the first night (oops!) but returned to our room the next day-after shopping!- to find that these had all been restocked. The bar area in the hotel recpetion was lovely...cosy fireplace and christmas tree! There are also lots of free drinks availible here...as well as snacks such as nuts/olives/cheeses etc.  Overall we had a great time and found the hotel very welcoming and a lovely place to hang around in both during the day and at night. It is a little expensive though worth it for a treat! The only thing we thought it could improve on was food...maybe restaurant or room service could be offered?

<Author>Search4Paradise
<Content>Excellent central Boutique Hotel with ' at home' experience Quick version - this is THE hotel to stay at in Amsterdam, book it if you like quality finishes and easy access. The quality and extra features (breakfast, all drinks, snacks) easily make up for the slight increase in cost over other hotels. Longer version - My wife and I spent my 30th Birthday at the Banks Mansion hotel and had a fantastic time. We used Trip Advisor for reviews and advice of where to stay so thanks to all for taking the time to comment. Although we have been to Amsterdam twice before, both stays right next to Dam Square, we wanted a quality hotel with attention to detail whilst being central enough to get around to the sites easily.We booked direct through the hotel鈥檚 website (cheaper than Expedia etc) received confirmation promptly and any requests were confirmed upon providing a credit card number.Looking at the map it appears that Banks Mansion is a little far from the attractions 鈥?but once you get there and take a look at the map you realise you could not be in a better location. You are simply right in the middle of the most popular areas - the Dam Square area to the north where you will find the tourist spots of Red Light District, souvenir shops, Madame Tussauds, coffee shops etc; East to the Artis zoo, the Leidesplein to the South West (restaurants etc) and then South to the Reiks Museum, Van Gogh museum and Heineken Experience. Oh and you are 50 yards from the flower market and the Rembrandtplein.Banks really is in the right spot - central AND quiet - it is in the old finance and lawyers district which means beautiful old historic bank buildings in traditional Dutch fashion, and is right on the canal.It took us 15 minutes to amble down the Damrak and Rokin taking in the sites and to arrive at the corner plot of the Banks Mansion with a decadent entrance warming you to the fact that you have chosen wisely ;o)Check in was easy and an upgrade to a small suite was offered to celebrate my birthday. Note in no way has the upgrade swung my vote on this hotel as it is so much more than that. The suite was on the ground floor and was a great size. More importantly the decor was just right, comfy and plush with clever lighting. Massive 7 foot square bed, 2 arm chairs, widescreen TV and DVD, large desk/dresser, Private Bar, lots of storage space in pretty art deco wardrobe, separate toilet and a big bathroom with deep bath and a separate, powerful rain fall shower. The BIG benefit of this hotel is the 'At Home' experience. So rather than spending a nice day seeing the attractions of Amsterdam and then coming back to your hotel and crashing out in your room and watching TV, waiting to go out not wanting to spend money on the mini-bar and not wanting to go to a bar just yet, here at Banks you can come back, dump your coat and chill out in the large lounge area with free self serve drinks and snacks. Every drink you could ask for is here including branded spirits in decanters, bottle beers, coffee machine and soft drinks. Snacks consisted of sushi, expensive nuts, pesto and bread. Just enough to get your appetite going for a nice meal out and plenty of magazines and papers to recommend the best nights (and days) out. In case you were wondering 鈥?does a free bar mean everyone gets wrecked 鈥?Not whilst we were there, it seems the hotel attracts the right type of guest who has better things to do than abuse a great feature of the hotel.So we ate at the Indonesian across the road (very tasty), Ocho's a Brazilian Grill near Leidesplein (great steaks) and Bangkok, a Thai recommended by the hotel again round the corner (which was very good and very popular with the locals - worth booking).Breakfast in the hotel is very good, full continental selection plus fruit, pancakes and the staple eggs, bacon and sausages (cooked well for a change) 鈥?plenty to get you through and avoid the need for lunch.If you are not a great lover of walking then a cab (hotel ordered us a very nice Mercedes MPV with chauffer) to the train station is less than 10 Euros perhaps a normal cab is even cheaper, and there is a Tram stop 50 metres from the hotel. But as the city is flat and there is so much to look at and take in I would strongly recommend an amble around this interesting city.For a third trip to Amsterdam this hotel served us incredibly well. We wanted something different (stayed in the Swissotel before which although pleasant is not even in the same league as Banks Mansion), something with a bit more attention and thought whilst still being affordable and within easy reach of the sites.We found it all in the Banks Mansion and would not hesitate recommending it for couples, business trips or small groups of friends. There is no point staying anywhere else in Amsterdam, perhaps it will be harder to get availability next time!

<Author>pauliepaul10
<Content>Superb Botique Hotel Well...after everything else that has been written about Banks Mansion, I think all we can do is agree say you should stay here if in Amsterdam!Banks Mansion lies in an extremely convenient location, just outside of the main shopping area and a minutes walk from the Flower Market. We walked from Central Station to the hotel when we arrived and it only took us 20 minutes (not walking particularly fast either) to get there. The hotel is virtually in a straight line from the station and could not have been easier to find. It was very easy to get back to the hotel from any direction in order to freshen up and grab a quick coffee during the day.From arrival to departure, all members of staff were extremely courteous and wanting to make your stay as pleasant as possible. On our day of departure we had left our luggage at the hotel whilst we enjoyed our last few hours in the city. When we returned to collect them at the end of the day, we were welcomed to enjoy one last drink from the house bar and to relax before departing for the airport.The rooms were of a first class quality and suprisingly big for European standards. As other reviewers have mentioned, everything is included in the price of the room, even the minibar in the room. What gave it that extra touch is that there were decanters in the room containing three different spirits to choose from and mixers in the fridge, rather than spirits in little plastic bottles!! Our room looked out onto the Herengracht canal and had windows that opened right up. Gave a lovely feel to the room.The only thing about our room was the cold tap on the shower...it had a tendancy to turn itself off slowly, making the water extremely hot! We would, without a doubt, stay at this hotel again. In fact, we are hoping to go back later this year and will be sure to contact the hotel for their availablilty and price.If you want an all inclusive hotel room, in a great location, with attentive staff, attractive art deco features and a friendly atmosphere, then definately choose Banks Mansion.

<Content>Just Like Home I am still staying in the Banks Mansion as I write this using the free Internet access and having a drink from the Free Bar too! These are just two of the things that make staying here a great experience.The Banks is an old converted merchants house by the Herengracht. The hotel is all done in an Art Deco style which only adds to the experience.My friends are staying here too and we all agree that we really like this hotel.Some of the rooms have a bath and some like mine have a shower. I am more of a shower person so this suits me but you can always specify which you prefer when you book. I was also allocated a non-smoking room which is great.One great thing about my shower is that it has a steamer built in with a eucalyptus oil option. I was out last night and found the smoke bothered me a bit so I was bunged up in my nose today. I just put on the steam room amd then sat in it for ten minutes and found this to be a great help.The buffet breakfast is very extensive too with both hot and cold items available.The staff are all very courteous and helpful.Overall I would have to say this hotel wins out because of the location, staff and overall standard of service offered. The rooms are all a decent size too which is a plus in Amsterdam as old buildings tend to have small rooms

<Author>MrandMrsTee
<Content>An excellent choice and an excellent value!! I agree with the reviewers who liked Banks Mansion. It is an excellent value - we got a relatively low rate directly though the hotel, and were very happy with a canal view room that was quiet if the windows were closed. We found the staff very helpful and nice, the room was narrow but decent in size and very nice in decor and furnishings (art deco look, with a big bathroom), particularly for Europe where narrow and eclectic rooms are typical even in more expensive hotels. The room was charming, if you like contemporary and spare European sensibilities.There were a lot of amenities included with the room (free in-room mini-bar, free alcohol in room and in lobby, inlcuding bottled beer and soft drinks, free snacks, complimentary breakfast which did include custom egg and waffle making, etc.) -- all of which was quite excellent and unique in our experience for any contemporary hotel in the US or Europe -- they are simply not out to strip you of every dime you bring in this place. With the decent nightly rate (180E for the two of us), for a canal view room and all of the amenities, we thought it was an excellent value.The hotel is extremely well located, in the central part of the canal belt near the Amstel River, the Rembrandtpelin and the flower market, yet its not too inner city (where it can get a little sleazy). It was a 5 minute or less walk to the Joordan, the Spui, Dam Square, Leidseplein and the Museum area. It's very close to Tempo Doloe and other excellent Indonesian restuarants, several of our favorite coffee shops (Damkring, Rokerij and Tweede Kamer), 2 or 3 trolley lines within a block of the front door, so it is ultra-convenient. This is a relaxed hotel with a relaxed attitude in an excellent location. We have stayed in hotels in Amsrterdam where we felt ever so slightly unwelcome, but not here. I guess I can understand how some people might find it underwhelming, but we really liked the combination of location, value and amenities. We will definitely stay here again when we come to Amsterdam.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fab weekend in Amsterdam at Banks Mansion ! I'm just back from a fab weekend in Amsterdam at a newish 4* hotel called Banks Mansion - it was very much to be recommended (with amazing free bar in the lounge and free booze in the room). We booked through lastminute and the rate was about GBP330 including breakfast, tax and service for 2 nights.Amsterdam was especially pretty decked out in Xmas decorations. Went to the Rijksmuseum (very good although part of collection was in storage due to building renovations), Van Gogh museum (excellent and you can buy your tickets at the hotel desk), Anne Frank house (interesting in a macabre way), and walked through the flower market (pretty) and red light district (strange!).We found several good restaurants, mainly informal places in the neighborhood where we were staying (Grachtengordel south) such as the Piet de Leeuw steakhouse which is a couple of blocks from the hotel, and one on Egelentiersstraat in Jordaan that was great because it had live music - called Claes Claesz. I also recommend the newly published (July 2005) Rough Guide to Amsterdam.I'll definitely be going back to Banks Mansion.Have a great trip!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Excellent Choice My husband and I stayed here Dec 2nd  3rd 2005. This was a really great choice of hotel - literally 5 mins walk from great shopping in Kalver-straat and Flower Market, 10 mins from Dam Square, with the option of heading down to the Jordann in the evening for bars/food etc., if you don't fancy the centre of town. We had a deluxe double, which although slightly dark at back of hotel, was immaculately appointed, huge bathroom, fab shower, minibar well stocked, and any drink you didn't have in your room was readily available in the free drinks area in the lobby. The self-service lounge/lobby area is a fab idea, and you can even get a cappucino and danish in the morning if you miss breakfast! If you've never been to Amsterdam before make a canal cruise and a trip to La Place Mangerie for food [5 mins from hotel; but closes @8pm], must-do's as part of your stay. There's also a good chinese directly across the road. We have already been raving about this hotel to our friends as the place in Amsterdam to stay and worth the cost.

<Content>Banks Mansion an amazing hotel My partner and I stayed at the Banks Mansion in July - this was our second stay at this amazing hotel. We will definitely be back in Amsterdam and certainly will stay at the Banks Mansion.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>What's not to like? Got a good deal via an Internet site for my first trip to Amsterdam, and was very satisfied indeed with the Banks Mansion. Very conveniently located in the attractive Grachtengordel area on one of Amsterdam's finest canals (Herrengracht), and only a short walk from the Vondelpark, Rijksmuseum, old town centre, flower market and Rembrandtsplein. Tram stop very close by for those who wish to go further afield.The hotel is Art Deco and nicely furnished; contemporary design style room was absolutely fine with comfortable bed, good bathroom, flat-screen TV, free minibar; the public area including the lounge also featured free food and drinks; the breakfast room (and breakfast) also perfectly acceptable. Staff were friendly and service was good.Really can't understand why anyone would be unhappy with the place; enjoyed a great stay and would recommend to anyone. It may not be 5 star but it's certainly a very good 4 star. Would definitely stay there again when I next visit Amsterdam.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A Splendid Hotel I am sorry for the previous reviewer who ended up with an unsatisfactory room, but I have to agree with the majority and say that my perception last weekend was of a friendly and welcoming place. I have a weakness for Art Nouveau and Art Deco and so I very much liked the decor of this splendid hotel-others might find it a bit over the top. The desk and waiting staff were helpful and efficient and everything was spotlessly clean. The bedroom and bathroom were both of a good size (my room had a pleasant outlook onto the Herengracht) and the power-shower was much appreciated. I made little use of the flat screen TV, DVD/CD player or free computer access but it was nice to know that they were there.The free bar (and free mini-bar in each room) is an excellent idea-the extortionate mini-bar prices in most hotels are a regular source of irritation-and I did not see anyone the worse for these facilities, though obviously someone with a weakness in that direction would do better to stay elsewhere. The breakfast was ample and served in an agreeable room with a relaxing atmosphere.The hotel's location is convenient for most parts of the city centre. I think that it offers good value for money in its price range and I look forward to staying there again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Style over Substance This was undoubtably the most disappointing, but not the worst, hotel I have ever visited. It touts its style and free bar but falls down on the basics. The rooms on the ground floor, we were lucky enough to catch two of them, are literally 2 metres from the pavement and three from the trams. Despite the double glazing there was far too much noise from both outside the hotel and inside from the reception area.The rooms themselves were constantly gloomy and the hotel doesn't seem to be able to afford lighting above 25 watts. One room, 008, is so small the wardrobe door only opens 45 degrees and the bathroom is so small you have to sit on the toilet sideways! The water is constantly boiling and with cold water taps in the shower that slowly turn themselves off, it makes for interesting bath times.The breakfast is merely adequate, not what you expect at 210 euros per person per night. There is a free bar and 2 computer terminals that are free to use but that in no way makes up in the deficencies of this hotel. Most of the small team of staff are pleasant, the leas helpful being the Genaral Manager who showed no interest in offering an alternative room. If you haven't booked, don't, there are far better hotels in this price category, if we hadn't paid in full before arrival we would have walked out, something I have only done once before in neraly 30 years of travelling on business and pleasure.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great weekend - Feb 05 Good hotel, good location.A bit worried about our room on 1st impression (smallish, ground floor, on street) but v comfortable and no problem from street noise.The concept here from the operators is clearly to spend cash on the decor, fittings etc and chuck in things like free room drinks and bar but save on the staffing; usually there was one receptionsist who doubled up making sure the bar was stocked with drinks and nibbles, and a guy who came round clearing up empty glasses etc and that's all the 'front of house' staff there were. Plus no restaurant apart from breakfast. I think on the whole it works, although it is dependent on the quality of what staff there are. One receptionist was very pleasant and helpful, the other less so, although both very knowledgeable, and you should definitely go to the Dutch restaurant they recommend round the corner. Mustard soup - fantastic!I would definitely go again.

<Author>ridina
<Content>Completely Fantastic! Went to Banks Mansion at the end of January 2005, and it was the perfect choice. The friendly and capable staff knew all the best places to go in the area. The breakfast was wonderful and free! You could order your pancakes or omelette to go with your toast, cereal, sausages, eggs and bacon- the works! The free bar in the room, and the open bar in the lounge meant that you could have a few drinks before going out (or coming back in!), and there was always something to nibble on. Not only were the beds super comfortable, which made it a real effort to wake up in the mornings, but they even had a pillow menu so you could choose your pillow. The shower/steam room with eucalyptus was very soothing and relaxing after a hard day's shopping. The location was excellent - the Dam square is only a 10 minute walk away. I would definitely go back!!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Average - rooms not that clean We picked this hotel because we'd read good reviews. It's not cheap and we didn't go for the basic room. The first thing we noticed was that the room was not that clean, the bathroom bin was not emptied ( and was full of horrible things) and we only had a tiny bit of toilet roll!!!!We didn't get the slippers that the website says you get and whilst the fridge in the room was restocked they didn't replace the things we drank most of - diet coke!. The toilet roll ration continued for the whole 4 nights - we ended up stealing some from the toilets in the bar. The free bar sounds good but .... we both drink red wine and would go out for an evening meal and a walk and arrived back about 10.30 to find no red wine left! They don't fill up the free bar quickly and if you happen to have people staying in the hotel who drink wine by the goldfish bowl - you've no chance! The walls of the rooms were also very thin, we were kept awake by the people next door who came in late and started on the mini bar. We also had a non smoking room that smelt of stale ciggies for the whole 4 nights, even our clothes smelt of it! The hotel is only ok -we didn't get back the extra price in the so called freebies! The breakfast was ok but by day 4 became boring! I'm not planning to stay here again - better bargains to be had. It's very close to he floating flower market (2 mins) if you are looking on the map - so the location is good (bur it's close to many cheaper hotels). I didn't find the staff that friendly either - although I did hear one of the receptionists sharing his drug experiences with another Brit - not my scene I'm afraid.

<Author>paullv
<Content>Would Stay There Again! I stayed at the Banks Mansion for 4 nights in November. I booked a deluxe room with Canal View but on my first night was given a nice room but with an alley view. I spoke to the staff at the front desk the next day and they moved me to a nicer room with a great canal view. I found the staff to be very friendly and helpful. The breakfast was good and made it so I was able to skip lunch since I was so full. I made good use of the mini bar in the lobby and met quite a few people there. The night clerk did close the mini bar very late (after 2 am) but I did not find this to be an issue. It was close enough to walk to everything and the neighborhood was very quiet late in the evening. The hotel website did state that internet was free. If you use your own laptop there is only 1/2 hour free during your stay and then the rest of the time you had to pay for access. There were two internet kiosks in the lobby that were always easily accessible and free. I booked this hotel based on the reviews here and I was very happy with my experience.

<Author>hodgeandpodge
<Content>Dont believe the hype! This hotel is not what you might expect from reviews and promos. The outside looks grey and worn and in need of a coat of paint. The bars on the outside windows give an institutional feel to the place and when you walk through the small revolving doors you can immediately notice the difference between a 4 and 5 star hotel no one to greet you or help with your baggage getting a large case through those small revolving doors must be an art form. The six hotel staff are pleasant yet inexperienced and unwilling to help with genuine problems. There are only 51 rooms in the hotel, if you are there its likely it will be fully booked so there is little play with your room. You get what youre given like it or lump. We reserved a deluxe room and were given a standard they then tried to pass this off as a deluxe but when checking friends that were staying at the hotel who had ordered the same room this clearly a standard/superior room, Do they think people are stupid? There is also a wide difference in the amount every one paid some people were unlucky enough to pay 250 euro per night some paid 98 euro no doubt for similar rooms. Food was also poor. When checking in they say the bar is open 24 hrs a day, this isnt true the night man closes it at 0200hrs. All in all Very expensive for what u get its not luxury I am a hotelier of 20 years and look back and laugh about this small hotel. We tried to check out within twenty minutes of arrival they charged 197 Euro......Money well spent
